Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais .iij. a cop.	And because of that they are the lighter cauterizations, because you make three in one blow.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the shoulder bone is displaced due to moisture and it is put back in place, but it cannot stay there and comes out again immediately upon a small movement that occurs, as we have observed, then it is necessary that you remove the initial displacement.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit; aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre; et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a .ij. ners douqueil ci est li forme:	Afterwards, have the patient lie on their back and on their side; afterwards, lift the knife that is inside the titillate ( possibly a tool used for this procedure) with your left hand; and if the joint is displaced inward, then heat the cautery that has two points, double-needle.
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble .iiij. cauteres; et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a .iij. ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres; et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a .iij. ners:	and cauterize the knife until it penetrates to the side, and the figure of the cautery will come together with 4 cauterizations; and that's why a cautery is made with the cautery that has 3 needles, because the shape of the cauterization are 6 cauterizations; and they are nerves according to the subtlety of a tent, and this is the form of the cautery that has 3 needles:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce .i. nerf por coi il i a .viij. cauteres.	And at no time is it added on top of those 3 nerves, which is why there are 6 cauterizations.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil; aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	Afterwards, put on the cauterized area a poultice made of cloth; afterwards, have the patient rest and do not move the limbs for a long time until they are well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated above, which can cause harm, then make a cautery above the thick part of the cautery handle, or many cauterizing needles that prick.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is refastened, and the moisture is removed, and the patient is healed.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When coldness and much moisture come into the stomach to the point where it strains him back to his complexion, and the patient has many cataracts, and in accustomed ways of treatment he does not benefit, then it is necessary that the patient be laid on their back, and stretch out their legs and hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture; et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	Then he makes three cauterizing needles I under the rib of the breast for the quantity of an egg yolk to the whole thickness of the handle, and two cauterizing needles on either side so that the shape of the cauterizing needles is at three angles, and there be this space between one and the other that they are not joined together when they spit out pus; and be the cauterizing needles so deep that they prick the two parts of the liver, and the shape of the cauterizing needles according to this form without adjustment.
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme; et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche; puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if you see that one must cauterize with a large cautery in the stomach according to this form; and he who has fear of this cautery, cauterize on pricking and marking above the stomach i point according to the size that you see by inch; then cauterize to the entire cautery which is called "point".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of the wound that we had previously treated, as long as they are healed.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez; et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil; et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient; et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi; et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere; et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez; et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais; et c’est li forme:	When the liver comes with pain of cold and moisture and heavy flatulence, as long as it is overfilled with its natural complexion by superfluities; and the patient is treated for what we have said in divisions, but does not benefit from it, then it behooves the patient to be seated on their heater; and mark an inch III cauteries according to this form and figure and quantity above the liver, below the ribs, where the flank of the belly comes; and there should be a space between each cautery the size of a thumb; and the cauteries should be as long as the body is long, and do not press your hand too much on all the cautery; and it should be burned so only half the kernel is blackened, and the patient should be straight up on their feet; and if they cannot, then sit down, stretch out their legs, and raise their arms; and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors; et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	And if your will is to, so cauterize these cauteries with a cauterizing iron, if you are subtle and wise in the art, and beware that you do not burn all through the flesh; for you would dry out all the body; and it should not come until just before the bowels, because the skin is very delicate at that place, and know this well for certain.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile: s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort; et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	When he has an abscess on the liver, and you want to know if it is in the flesh of the liver or in the membrane: if it is in the flesh, the patient feels pain but not too much; and if it is in the membrane, he feels pain beyond measure.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste; et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	And then when the treatment of the cure required mirrors, it is necessary that the patient be raised above his head; and then mark out with a needle the place where the abscess is, and then heat the cauterizing iron which is similar to the sun, from whose shape this form is.
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers; aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez; et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	And burn with fire cautery until the blisters are burned, and come to a scab, so that the pus is completely purged; then treat according to the treatment of ulcers until they are healed; and it does not seem right for anyone who has not studied medicine for a long time, and by whose hands these diseases have been cured sometimes.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Then it can be boldly done, and I think that it is better to leave him alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	of the cautery for pleurisy (a type of inflammation or irritation of the lining surrounding the lungs)
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere: pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois; et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize .i. cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et .ij. petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe; et .ij. cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc; et .i. cautere emmi le pis, et .i. autre sus l’estomac, et .i. entre .ij. espaules, et .ij. as .ij. costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre .ij. espaules; et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	The ancient ones said that for pleurisy, one should make cauterizations with roots of aristolochia (a plant), and in this manner: take a long root of aristolochia, the longest you can find, and dry it out, and as thick and as long as your thumb; then wet it in oil, and grasp it by the fire, and cauterize one cautery between the ribcage and the neck, and two small cauteries a little lower down in the part that is below the beard; and two cauteries between the fifth rib and the sixth, going downward behind a little; and one cautery in the middle of the chest, and another on top of the stomach, and one between the two shoulders, and two others at the two sides of the chest below the cautery that is between the two shoulders; and do not press your hand down, but rather pull it back out openly like a scenting.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme; et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	And some ancient said that one should use the fire cautery resembling a razor, and heat it and put it between the ribs, so long as it comes to the abscess; and the pain bursts forth, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear for the patient's death now, or a fistula comes which cannot be healed.
